# Text Elements
- Has a giant molecular structure
- All are covelantly bonded/ Strong bonds ^GIk2qMXa

We can do a displacement reaction, Cl2 reacts with NaI, 
Displacing Iodine, while I2 cannot displace Chlorine from NaCl

-> Cl2 + NaI -> NaCl + I2
Vapours of a purpullish solid forms ^2cHwXKh7
